!Series_title	"CIRCULATING MICRORNAs PREDICT SURVIVAL OF PATIENTS WITH TUMORS OF GLIAL ORIGIN"
!Series_geo_accession	"GSE112462"
!Series_status	"Public on Mar 29 2018"
!Series_submission_date	"Mar 28 2018"
!Series_last_update_date	"Jul 03 2018"
!Series_pubmed_id	"29643013"
!Series_web_link	"https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/?term=29643013"
!Series_summary	"We analyzed serum extracellular vescicles (SEV) of 28 patients with glioma tumors and 8 normal samples by Nanostring, and validated a microRNA profile that can differentiate between and among some classes of CNS tumors."
!Series_overall_design	"A total of 28 glial tumor SEV samples were collected from UCFS, and 8 SEV normal control samples from The Ohio State University, Columbus, OH."

!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1	"Extracellular vesicles were extracted from 250μl of serum using Exoquick plus (System Bioscience cat#EXOQ5TM-1) and following manufacturer instructions. The exosomal pellet resuspended in  1,5 ml of TRIReagent (SIGMA-ALDRICH cat#T9424-200ml), and  2μl of 33.3 attoMole solution of spike-ins (cel-miR-248 and ath-miR159a) were added to each sample. Manufacturer instructions were followed up to the isolation of the acqueous phase. An equal volume of 70% ETOH was added to the acqueous phase, and loaded to the columns of the NORGEN RNA Clean-up and Concentration kit (cat#23600) and RNA was isolated following manufacturer instructions."
